                            if (!browsersVersions || Object.keys(browsersVersions).length === 0) {

                                    { name: 'chrome', pattern: /(chrome)\/([\d]+)/i },
                                    { name: 'firefox', pattern: /(firefox)\/([\d]+)/i },
                                    { name: 'safari', pattern: /(version)\/([\d]+).*?(safari)/i },
